***скупой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупо́й</a> (11280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">скупъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skupŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skǫpъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skupój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скупе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скупе́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>avaricious, stingy, frugal, mean, parsimonious, miserly</li>
<li>scanty, poor</li>
<li>taciturn</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прижимистый.html>прижи́мистый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prižimistyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ска́редный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skárednyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедный.html>бе́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bédnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skúdnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержать.html>сде́ржанный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sdéržannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умеренный.html>уме́ренный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">umérennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skupój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупо́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупы́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупы́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупа́я</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>miser</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скупость.html>ску́пость</a> (23096)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупой.html>скупо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skupój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупость.html>ску́пость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skúpostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупость.html>ску́пости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупость.html>ску́пости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупость.html>ску́постей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скучать.html>скуча́ть</a> (4589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скучать.html>скуча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skučátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be bored</li>
<li>to long for, to miss <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative or prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скучать.html>скуча́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>skučáju</b> po tebé</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I miss you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ску<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:участник.html>Уча́стники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:описываемый.html>опи́сываемой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощью</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:скучать.html>скуча́ть</a></i>: <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:субъект.html>субъект</a> (им. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объект</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> + <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́т</a>. п. / <a href = vnd.unilang:пред.html>пред</a>. п. (<span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">устар.</span>)).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-скуч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***скучный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скучный.html>ску́чный</a> (4217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скука.html>ску́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skúka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скучный.html>ску́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skúšnyj, skúčnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скучне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скучне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скучный.html>ску́чный</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скучнейший.html>скучне́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dull, boring, tedious, tiresome (inciting boredom)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скучный.html>ску́чен</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чера</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>ко́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skúčen/Skúšen</b> denʹ do véčera, kóli délatʹ néčevo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Day-by-day a day goes by.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">The day is boring until the evening if there's nothing to do.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bored, listless</li></ol>

***скушать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скушать.html>ску́шать</a> (20366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушать.html>ку́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скушать.html>ску́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skúšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушать.html>ку́шать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to eat, to have, to take</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swallow, to pocket
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скушать.html>ску́шать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обида.html>оби́ду</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:оскорбление.html>оскорбле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skúšatʹ</b> obídu/oskorblénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to swallow/pocket an insult</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat up, to buy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>скажи́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скушать.html>ску́шает</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú što ni skaží, on vsjó <b>skúšajet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he will buy [eat up] whatever you tell him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat up, to ruin</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушанье.html>ку́шанье</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kúšanʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><b>ску́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шать</b>

<p>Perhaps <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slábyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slábyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-iná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slack

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> weak point, weak spot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слабина.html>слабину́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ <b>slabinú</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show weakness; give in</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабоумный.html>слабоу́мный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slaboúmnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>imbecile, weakheaded, weakminded, feeble-minded, soft in the head</li></ol>

<p><b>сла<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>у́м</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***слабый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бый</a> (860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slabъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slábyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)слабе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:слабеть.html>слабе́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">слабе́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>weak, feeble</li>
<li>faint</li>
<li>infirm</li>
<li>delicate</li>
<li>flabby</li>
<li>poor</li></ol>

<p><b>сла́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бый</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-слаб-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***слава.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> (863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slàva</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sláva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>сла́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>glory
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́гу</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sláva bógu!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">glory be to God!; thank God!;</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na slávu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">first-rate; A-one; excellent</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ву</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo <b>slávu</b> pobédy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to the glory of victory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:герой.html>геро́ям</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sláva</b> gerójam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">glory to the heroes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fame, renown</li>
<li>repute, reputation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>дурна́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">durnája sláva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">notoriety; ill repute</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rumour, rumor</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славить.html>сла́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прославить.html>просла́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to praise, to glorify, to laud, to extol</li></ol>

<ol><li>to be famous <i>(for)</i>, to be famed <i>(for)</i>, to be renowned <i>(for)</i>, to have a reputation <i>(for)</i></li>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славить.html>сла́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:славить.html>сла́вленный</a> (20865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славить.html>сла́вленный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slávlennyj</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:славословие.html>славосло́вие</a> (30437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sláva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slóvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славословие.html>славосло́вие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slavoslóvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славословие.html>славосло́вия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славословие.html>славосло́вия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славословие.html>славосло́вий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> glorification, adulation <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially of God</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, doxology</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> immoderate praise, flattery</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:славянин.html>славяни́н</a> (11748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">словѣнинъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slověninŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slověninъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Slav</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Further etymology is disputed.
</p>

<p><b>сла<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сложить.html>сложи́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лаг-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
